[30;1m17 | [0m[35m* So we should choose a media-breakpoint-down one *lower* than when we want to start[0m
[30;1m18 | [0m[35m* example: media-breakpoint-up(md) and media-breakpoint-down(sm) trigger at the same time[0m

[30;1m20 | [0m[35m*/[0m

[30;1m22 | [0m[35m$breakpoint-sidebar-secondary: xl; // When we collapse the secondary sidebar[0m
